    SELECT r."Id", r."AssignedWaiterId", r."Capacity", r."CreatedAt", r."IsDeleted", r."QrIdentifier", r."Status", r."TableNumber", u."Id" AS "Id0", u."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", u."EncryptedMobileNumber", u."HashKey", u."IsActive", u."IsDeleted" AS "IsDeleted0", u."MobileNumberHash", u."MustChangePassword", u."Name", u."PasswordHash", u."Role", u."Username"
    FROM "RestaurantTables" AS r
    LEFT JOIN "Users" AS u ON r."AssignedWaiterId" = u."Id"
    WHERE r."Id" = @__tableId_0 AND NOT (r."IsDeleted")
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "DiningSessions" AS d ON t."Id" = d."TableId"
ORDER BY t."Id", t."Id0"
